msg:I visited relatives on the second day of the Chinese New Year and chose a hotel close to my relatives' home. The stay experience was great. Next time I come to Changzhou, I will choose Wyndham Garden Hotel.

The Spring Festival price is only about 100 yuan more expensive than the usual price, which is very conscientious. The young man who checked in was very enthusiastic. Seeing that we had a lot of luggage, he took the initiative to take the cart to help us go up.

The room is on the 9th floor, spacious and bright, clean and sanitary, with good sound insulation, and the bed is also very comfortable. I also gave fruit snacks and New Year red envelopes, and the cleaning aunt was also very enthusiastic.

The buffet breakfast is quite rich, and every staff member is very enthusiastic, especially üëçAn aunt saw that our baby didn't like to eat, so she helped us order a bowl of wontons. Another waiter brought the freshly baked egg yolk cake. The baby of a guest next to him was naughty while eating and accidentally knocked over the plate. The waiter didn't blame him at all, and sent a clean towel to the guest to wipe his clothes. He patiently cleaned the floor with a mop and called the cleaning aunt to wipe the floor again. Breakfast ends at 10 o'clock. At 10:30, the waiter reminds everyone whether they want to take more food, giving the late guests enough time to eat.

It is also very convenient to drive to the China Dinosaur Park for half an hour. Arrive before the park opens at 9 o'clock. There are few people when you first enter the park, and you don't need to queue for many projects. It takes a long time to queue after 10 o'clock. The indoor roller coaster queues for 3 hours.
